The opposite of a narrow ruling is broad or sweeping. If you want to describe the vote outcome as narrow (as in a narrow victory, I suppose?), then the opposite is unanimous.
SCOTUS majority in a case can be 5-4, 7-2, 9-0, whatever. Okay, that's done. Now, what did that majority decide? The same outcome can be narrow (applies to that one case only) or sweeping (applies to all cases of that type).
